      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_lunar_eclipses_between_1001_and_1100">
        List of lunar eclipses between 1001 and 1100
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_11th-century_lunar_eclipses&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of lunar eclipses between 1001 and 1100">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There were 246 lunar eclipse events between 1001 and 1100 CE
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

            <li>
             <img alt="Portal" data-file-height="28" data-file-width="32" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/16px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/24px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fd/Portal-puzzle.svg/32px-Portal-puzzle.svg.png 2x" title="Portal" width="16"/>
             <a href="/wiki/Portal:Moon" title="Portal:Moon">
              Portal
             </a>
            </li>
            <li>
             <img alt="WikiProject" data-file-height="100" data-file-width="100" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/16px-People_icon.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/24px-People_icon.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/People_icon.svg/32px-People_icon.svg.png 2x" title="WikiProject" width="16"/>
             <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:WikiProject_Eclipses" title="Wikipedia:WikiProject Eclipses">
              WikiProject
             </a>
            </li>
            <li>
             <span style="background-color: #FC6">
              →
             </span>
             <small>
              symbol denotes next eclipse in series
             </small>
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
         </td>
        </tr>
       </table>
      </div>
